{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type $>$ \\
Value\+Type Poco\+::\+Any\+Cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{operand }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Any\+Cast operator used to extract a copy of the Value\+Type from an \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}}\&.

Example Usage\+: My\+Type tmp = Any\+Cast$<$\+My\+Type$>$(an\+Any). Will throw a Bad\+Cast\+Exception if the cast fails. Dont use an Any\+Cast in combination with references, i.\+e. My\+Type\& tmp = ... or const My\+Type\& tmp = ... Some compilers will accept this code although a copy is returned. Use the Ref\+Any\+Cast in these cases.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{format()}{format()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::string \mbox{\hyperlink{Foundation_8h_aa8ac83d4c3361414b6d5fcb37a7eb1ce}{Foundation\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} Poco\+::format (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{fmt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacePoco_a249499455c6080fe66e8248856850cd2}\label{namespacePoco_a249499455c6080fe66e8248856850cd2}} 
\index{Poco@{Poco}!format@{format}}
\index{format@{format}!Poco@{Poco}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{format()}{format()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/21]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::string \mbox{\hyperlink{Foundation_8h_aa8ac83d4c3361414b6d5fcb37a7eb1ce}{Foundation\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} Poco\+::format (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{fmt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{value1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{value2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function implements sprintf-\/style formatting in a typesafe way. Various variants of the function are available, supporting a different number of arguments (up to six).

The formatting is controlled by the format string in fmt. Format strings are quite similar to those of the std\+::printf() function, but there are some minor differences.

The format string can consist of any sequence of characters; certain characters have a special meaning. Characters without a special meaning are copied verbatim to the result. A percent sign (\%) marks the beginning of a format specification. Format specifications have the following syntax\+:

\%\mbox{[}$<$index$>$\mbox{]}\mbox{[}$<$flags$>$\mbox{]}\mbox{[}$<$width$>$\mbox{]}\mbox{[}.$<$precision$>$\mbox{]}\mbox{[}$<$modifier$>$\mbox{]}$<$type$>$

Index, flags, width, precision and prefix are optional. The only required part of the format specification, apart from the percent sign, is the type.

The optional index argument has the format \char`\"{}\mbox{[}$<$n$>$\mbox{]}\char`\"{} and allows to address an argument by its zero-\/based position (see the example below).

Following are valid type specifications and their meaning\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item b boolean (true = 1, false = 0)
\item c character
\item d signed decimal integer
\item i signed decimal integer
\item o unsigned octal integer
\item u unsigned decimal integer
\item x unsigned hexadecimal integer (lower case)
\item X unsigned hexadecimal integer (upper case)
\item e signed floating-\/point value in the form \mbox{[}-\/\mbox{]}d.\+dddde\mbox{[}$<$sign$>$\mbox{]}dd\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}
\item E signed floating-\/point value in the form \mbox{[}-\/\mbox{]}d.\+ddddE\mbox{[}$<$sign$>$\mbox{]}dd\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}
\item f signed floating-\/point value in the form \mbox{[}-\/\mbox{]}dddd.\+dddd
\item s std\+::string
\item z std\+::size\+\_\+t
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following flags are supported\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/ left align the result within the given field width
\item + prefix the output value with a sign (+ or -\/) if the output value is of a signed type
\item 0 if width is prefixed with 0, zeros are added until the minimum width is reached
\item \# For o, x, X, the \# flag prefixes any nonzero output value with 0, 0x, or 0X, respectively; for e, E, f, the \# flag forces the output value to contain a decimal point in all cases.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following modifiers are supported\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item (none) argument is char (c), int (d, i), unsigned (o, u, x, X) double (e, E, f, g, G) or string (s)
\item l argument is long (d, i), unsigned long (o, u, x, X) or long double (e, E, f, g, G)
\item L argument is long long (d, i), unsigned long long (o, u, x, X)
\item h argument is short (d, i), unsigned short (o, u, x, X) or float (e, E, f, g, G)
\item ? argument is any signed or unsigned int, short, long, or 64-\/bit integer (d, i, o, x, X)
\end{DoxyItemize}

The width argument is a nonnegative decimal integer controlling the minimum number of characters printed. If the number of characters in the output value is less than the specified width, blanks or leading zeros are added, according to the specified flags (-\/, +, 0).

Precision is a nonnegative decimal integer, preceded by a period (.), which specifies the number of characters to be printed, the number of decimal places, or the number of significant digits.

Throws an Invalid\+Argument\+Exception if an argument index is out of range.

Starting with release 1.\+4.\+3, an argument that does not match the format specifier no longer results in a Bad\+Cast\+Exception. The string \mbox{[}E\+R\+R\+F\+MT\mbox{]} is written to the result string instead.

If there are more format specifiers than values, the format specifiers without a corresponding value are copied verbatim to output.

If there are more values than format specifiers, the superfluous values are ignored.

Usage Examples\+: std\+::string s1 = format(\char`\"{}\+The answer to life, the universe, and everything is \%d\char`\"{}, 42); std\+::string s2 = format(\char`\"{}second\+: \%\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}d, first\+: \%\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}d\char`\"{}, 1, 2); \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacePoco_a1257924cfd2f9ec28b1c094d26c41ae2}\label{namespacePoco_a1257924cfd2f9ec28b1c094d26c41ae2}}

Here is the call graph for this function\+:
% FIG 18
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacePoco_ac960e70625c222e94b4b6f559248d441}\label{namespacePoco_ac960e70625c222e94b4b6f559248d441}} 
\index{Poco@{Poco}!intToStr@{intToStr}}
\index{intToStr@{intToStr}!Poco@{Poco}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intToStr()}{intToStr()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
bool Poco\+::int\+To\+Str (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{value,  }\item[{unsigned short}]{base,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{result,  }\item[{std\+::size\+\_\+t \&}]{size,  }\item[{bool}]{prefix = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{char}]{fill = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}~\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{char}]{th\+Sep = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts integer to string. Numeric bases from binary to hexadecimal are supported. If width is non-\/zero, it pads the return value with fill character to the specified width. When padding is zero character (\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}), it is prepended to the number itself; all other paddings are prepended to the formatted result with minus sign or base prefix included If prefix is true and base is octal or hexadecimal, respective prefix (\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{} for octal, \char`\"{}0x\char`\"{} for hexadecimal) is prepended. For all other bases, prefix argument is ignored. Formatted string has at least \mbox{[}width\mbox{]} total length.

% FIG 79
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacePoco_a634a717db18c7880d10a2753077a1a25}\label{namespacePoco_a634a717db18c7880d10a2753077a1a25}} 
\index{Poco@{Poco}!uIntToStr@{uIntToStr}}
\index{uIntToStr@{uIntToStr}!Poco@{Poco}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uIntToStr()}{uIntToStr()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
bool Poco\+::u\+Int\+To\+Str (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{value,  }\item[{unsigned short}]{base,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{result,  }\item[{std\+::size\+\_\+t \&}]{size,  }\item[{bool}]{prefix = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{char}]{fill = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}~\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{char}]{th\+Sep = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Converts unsigned integer to string. Numeric bases from binary to hexadecimal are supported. If width is non-\/zero, it pads the return value with fill character to the specified width. When padding is zero character (\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}), it is prepended to the number itself; all other paddings are prepended to the formatted result with minus sign or base prefix included If prefix is true and base is octal or hexadecimal, respective prefix (\textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{} for octal, \char`\"{}0x\char`\"{} for hexadecimal) is prepended. For all other bases, prefix argument is ignored. Formatted string has at least \mbox{[}width\mbox{]} total length. 

Definition at line 339 of file Numeric\+String.\+h.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UnsafeAnyCast()}{UnsafeAnyCast()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type $>$ \\
Value\+Type$\ast$ Poco\+::\+Unsafe\+Any\+Cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} $\ast$}]{operand }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The \char`\"{}unsafe\char`\"{} versions of Any\+Cast are not part of the public interface and may be removed at any time. They are required where we know what type is stored in the any and can\textquotesingle{}t use typeid() comparison, e.\+g., when our types may travel across different shared libraries.
